{
  "content": "---\nname: hivemind-skill-writer\ndescription: Use when creating, auditing, refactoring, or packaging HiveMind framework skills. Activates the meta-builder for skill authoring, TDD workflows, and quality validation. Bundles skill-writing guidance, Skill-Judge metrics, and HiveMind-specific packaging patterns.\nversion: 1.0.0\nframework: hivemind\npack: hivemind-skill-writer\nentry-level: L1\npattern: P1\nstacking: 0\nowner: hivemind\nstatus: active\n---\n\n# hivemind-skill-writer\n\n## Purpose\n\nMeta-builder skill for authoring HiveMind-specific skills. Use when you need to create, audit, refactor, or package skills for the HiveMind ecosystem.\n\n## When to Activate\n\n**Primary Triggers:**\n- User asks to create a new skill\n- User asks to audit existing skills\n- User asks to refactor skill structure\n- User asks to package skill sets\n- Intent involves skill authoring\n\n**Secondary Triggers:**\n- Detecting skill quality issues\n- Identifying skill redundancy\n- Planning skill migration\n\n## Core Philosophy\n\n### The Iron Law\n\n> **NO SKILL WITHOUT A FAILING TEST FIRST**\n\nEvery skill must be validated against a real failure scenario before being written.\n\n### Progressive Disclosure\n\n| Level | Content | When |\n|-------|---------|------|\n| **L1** | Metadata + overview | Always loaded (~100 words) |\n| **L2** | SKILL.md body | On trigger match (~500 lines) |\n| **L3** | Reference bundle | Explicit request |\n\n### The 3 Patterns\n\n**Pattern 1 — High-Level Routing**\n- Thin, must-load entry skills\n- Route to specialized sub-packs\n- Stacking: P1 + P2 or P1 + P3\n\n**Pattern 2 — Domain-Specific**\n- Deeper guidance for specific domains\n- Step-by-step with templates\n- Stacking: P2 standalone OR P1 + P2\n\n**Pattern 3 — Expertise Depth**\n- Vertical depth for complex scenarios\n- Activated when P1/P2 insufficient\n- Uses TOC + jump links\n\n## Skill Anatomy\n\nEvery HiveMind skill follows this structure:\n\n```\nskill-name/\n├── SKILL.md                    # Required entry\n├── references/                # L3 content\n│   ├── 01-topic-alpha.md     # Numbered for ordering\n│   ├── 02-topic-beta.md\n│   └── index.md              # TOC for P3\n├── scripts/                   # Discovery only\n│   └── detect-pattern.sh\n└── templates/                # Reusable\n    └── report-template.md\n```\n\n## Frontmatter Standard\n\n```yaml\n---\nname: skill-name-with-hyphens\ndescription: Use when [triggering conditions] — [effect] — [constraints]\nversion: 1.0.0\nframework: hivemind\npack: pack-name\nentry-level: L1|L2|L3\npattern: P1|P2|P3\nstacking: 0-3\nowner: hivemind\nstatus: active|deprecated|draft\n---\n```\n\n## TDD Workflow (RED-GREEN-REFACTOR)\n\n### RED Phase\n1. Identify the failing scenario\n2. Write test prompt for the scenario\n3. Run without skill — observe failure\n4. Document exact failure mode\n\n### GREEN Phase\n1. Write minimal skill addressing failure\n2. Run with skill — observe pass\n3. Verify failure mode resolved\n4. Document success criteria\n\n### REFACTOR Phase\n1. Remove duplication\n2. Tighten trigger accuracy\n3. Ensure reference depth compliance\n4. Validate stacking ≤3\n\n## Skill-Judge Quality Metrics\n\n| Dimension | Weight | Check |\n|-----------|--------|-------|\n| **Trigger Accuracy** | 25% | Description triggers on specific conditions |\n| **Action Coherence** | 25% | ONE thing well, no mission creep |\n| **Reference Integrity** | 20% | 1-level depth, no circular refs |\n| **Non-Redundancy** | 15% | No overlap with existing skills |\n| **Edge Case Coverage** | 15% | Handles degraded/delegated states |\n\n### Quality Thresholds\n\n| Score | Grade | Action |\n|-------|-------|--------|\n| 4.5+ | EXCELLENT | Ready for release |\n| 4.0+ | GOOD | Minor improvements |\n| 3.0+ | ACCEPTABLE | Address gaps |\n| <3.0 | NEEDS WORK | Major revision required |\n\n## Context-Intelligence Integration\n\nEvery skill must integrate with the context-intelligence pack:\n\n- **Entry State Recognition**: Acknowledge session state\n- **Trust Threshold**: Know minimum trust scores\n- **Rot Detection**: Watch for degradation signals\n- **Recovery Awareness**: Know when to escalate\n\n## Stacking Discipline\n\nAt entry, max **3 skills** may load:\n\n```\ncontext-intelligence (1) — always\ndelegation-scope (1) — if delegated\nworkflow-hierarchy (1) — if workflow\ncontext-rot-recovery (1) — if degraded\n```\n\n**hivemind-skill-writer does not count** against stack (stacking: 0).\n\n## References\n\n- `references/01-skill-anatomy.md` — Full anatomy template\n- `references/02-frontmatter-standard.md` — YAML schema\n- `references/03-three-patterns.md` — Pattern system details\n- `references/04-tdd-workflow.md` — TDD methodology\n- `references/05-skill-quality-matrix.md` — Skill-Judge metrics\n\n## Anti-Patterns\n\n**DO NOT:**\n- Create skills without failing test first\n- Use vague descriptions (\"Use when managing state\")\n- Exceed 1-level reference depth\n- Stack >3 skills at entry\n- Duplicate existing skill purposes\n- Force framework dogma over user intent\n\n**DO:**\n- Be specific in triggers (\"Use when delegation scope is ambiguous\")\n- Use progressive disclosure\n- Respect stacking limits\n- Integrate with context-intelligence\n- Follow the TDD workflow\n",
  "filePath": "/Users/apple/hivemind-plugin/skills/hivemind-skill-writer/SKILL.md"
}

  "content": "# Skill Anatomy Template\n\n## Purpose\n\nStandard structure for all HiveMind skills. Every skill must follow this anatomy.\n\n---\n\n## Required Elements\n\n### SKILL.md (Entry Point)\n\nEvery skill directory MUST have a `SKILL.md` at its root.\n\n```\nskill-name/\n└── SKILL.md                    # REQUIRED\n```\n\n### Minimum Frontmatter\n\n```yaml\n---\nname: skill-name-with-hyphens\ndescription: Use when [triggering conditions] — [effect]\nversion: 1.0.0\nframework: hivemind\npack: pack-name\nentry-level: L1|L2|L3\npattern: P1|P2|P3\nstacking: 0-3\nowner: hivemind\nstatus: active\n---\n```\n\n### Required Sections in SKILL.md\n\n1. **Purpose** — What the skill does (1-2 sentences)\n2. **When to Activate** — Specific trigger conditions\n3. **Core Behavior** — How it works\n4. **Anti-Patterns** — What NOT to do\n\n---\n\n## Optional Elements\n\n### references/\n\nFor P2 and P3 skills, create a `references/` directory:\n\n```\nskill-name/\n├── SKILL.md\n└── references/\n    ├── 01-topic-alpha.md\n    ├── 02-topic-beta.md\n    └── index.md          # TOC for P3\n```\n\n**Rules:**\n- Number files for ordering\n- One topic per file\n- 1-level depth MAX\n- P3 skills MUST have index.md with TOC + jump links\n\n### scripts/\n\nFor skills requiring discovery tooling:\n\n```\nskill-name/\n├── SKILL.md\n└── scripts/\n    └── detect-pattern.sh    # Discovery only\n```\n\n**Rules:**\n- Read-only by default\n- No mutation scripts\n- Safe for multi-environment\n\n### templates/\n\nFor reusable output formats:\n\n```\nskill-name/\n├── SKILL.md\n└── templates/\n    └── report-template.md\n```\n\n---\n\n## Pattern-Specific Requirements\n\n### P1 Skills (High-Level Routing)\n\n| Requirement | Specification |\n|-------------|---------------|\n| SKILL.md size | <200 lines |\n| Body | Route conditions only |\n| References | Optional |\n| Stacking | Typically 1 |\n\n**Example P1:**\n```markdown\n# Skill Name\n\n## Purpose\nThin routing skill that directs to specialized sub-packs.\n\n## When to Activate\n- Trigger A\n- Trigger B\n\n## Routing Logic\nIF condition A → load sub-pack-X\nIF condition B → load sub-pack-Y\n\n## References\n(references/ for detail)\n```\n\n### P2 Skills (Domain-Specific)\n\n| Requirement | Specification |\n|-------------|---------------|\n| SKILL.md size | 200-500 lines |\n| Body | Step-by-step guidance |\n| References | Required |\n| Templates | As needed |\n\n**Example P2:**\n```markdown\n# Skill Name\n\n## Purpose\nDomain-specific guidance for [area].\n\n## When to Activate\n- Trigger A\n- Trigger B\n\n## Step-by-Step Process\n\n### Step 1: [Name]\nDescription...\n\n### Step 2: [Name]\nDescription...\n\n## Templates\n(template link)\n\n## Anti-Patterns\n- What NOT to do\n```\n\n### P3 Skills (Expertise Depth)\n\n| Requirement | Specification |\n|-------------|---------------|\n| SKILL.md size | >500 lines OR |\n| Body | TOC + section targets |\n| References | Heavy bundle |\n| index.md | REQUIRED with jumps |\n\n**Example P3 Structure:**\n```markdown\n# Skill Name\n\n## Overview\n\n## Table of Contents\n- [Section A](#section-a)\n- [Section B](#section-b)\n- [Section C](#section-c)\n\n## Section A\nContent...\n\n## Section B\nContent...\n\n## Section C\nContent...\n\n---\n\n# References\n\n## Detailed Topic A\nHeavy content...\n\n## Detailed Topic B\nHeavy content...\n\n## index.md (TOC)\n(reference bundle TOC)\n```\n\n---\n\n## Naming Rules\n\n| Element | Format | Example |\n|---------|--------|---------|\n| Skill directory | kebab-case | `context-intelligence` |\n| SKILL.md | literal | `SKILL.md` |\n| Reference files | nn-name.md | `01-context-rot.md` |\n| TOC index | literal | `index.md` |\n| Scripts | kebab-case | `detect-pattern.sh` |\n| Templates | kebab-case | `report-template.md` |\n\n---\n\n## Version Policy\n\n| Change | Bump |\n|--------|------|\n| New trigger | MINOR |\n| Breaking trigger | MAJOR |\n| New reference | PATCH |\n| Bug fix | PATCH |\n\n---\n\n## Status Values\n\n| Status | Meaning |\n|--------|---------|\n| `active` | Ready for use |\n| `draft` | In development |\n| `deprecated` | Will be removed |\n| `archived` | Historical only |\n\n---\n\n## Integration Points\n\nEvery skill should document:\n\n1. **Parent Pack**: What pack does it belong to?\n2. **Entry Level**: When does it load?\n3. **Pattern**: P1/P2/P3?\n4. **Stacking**: How does it affect stack count?\n5. **Context Integration**: Does it use context-intelligence?\n",

{
  "content": "# Frontmatter Standard\n\n## Purpose\n\nYAML frontmatter schema for HiveMind skills. Every SKILL.md must have valid frontmatter.\n\n---\n\n## Complete Schema\n\n```yaml\n---\nname: skill-name-with-hyphens\ndescription: Use when [triggering conditions] — [effect] — [constraints]\nversion: 1.0.0\nframework: hivemind\npack: pack-name\nentry-level: L1|L2|L3\npattern: P1|P2|P3\nstacking: 0-3\nowner: hivemind\nstatus: active|deprecated|draft\ntags: [optional, tags]\ndepends-on: [optional, dependencies]\n---\n```\n\n---\n\n## Field Definitions\n\n### name (REQUIRED)\n\n**Type:** string  \n**Format:** kebab-case (lowercase with hyphens)\n\n```yaml\nname: context-intelligence\nname: delegation-scope\nname: context-rot-recovery\n```\n\n**Rules:**\n- Lowercase only\n- Hyphens between words\n- No numbers at start\n- Descriptive but concise\n\n### description (REQUIRED)\n\n**Type:** string  \n**Format:** \"Use when [conditions] — [effect] — [constraints]\"\n\n```yaml\ndescription: >\n  Use when starting a session, resuming after interruption,\n  detecting context drift, or when delegation scope is unclear.\n  Provides context rot defense and trust scoring.\n```\n\n**Rules:**\n- Start with \"Use when...\"\n- Include specific trigger conditions\n- Describe effect clearly\n- Add constraints if any\n- Max 500 characters\n- Third person perspective\n\n### version (REQUIRED)\n\n**Type:** string  \n**Format:** Semantic versioning (semver)\n\n```yaml\nversion: 1.0.0\nversion: 1.2.0\nversion: 2.0.0\n```\n\n**Semver Rules:**\n- MAJOR: Breaking trigger change\n- MINOR: New trigger added\n- PATCH: Bug fix, new reference\n\n### framework (REQUIRED)\n\n**Type:** string  \n**Value:** `hivemind`\n\n```yaml\nframework: hivemind\n```\n\n### pack (REQUIRED)\n\n**Type:** string  \n**Format:** Pack hierarchy\n\n```yaml\npack: context-intelligence\npack: context-intelligence/delegation\npack: hivemind-skill-writer\npack: explore\npack: general\n```\n\n### entry-level (REQUIRED)\n\n**Type:** string  \n**Values:** L1, L2, L3\n\n| Level | When | Size |\n|-------|------|------|\n| L1 | Always loaded at entry | ~100 words |\n| L2 | On trigger match | ~500 lines |\n| L3 | Explicit request | References |\n\n```yaml\nentry-level: L1   # Always loaded\nentry-level: L2   # On trigger\nentry-level: L3   # On explicit request\n```\n\n### pattern (REQUIRED)\n\n**Type:** string  \n**Values:** P1, P2, P3\n\n| Pattern | Purpose |\n|---------|---------|\n| P1 | High-level routing |\n| P2 | Domain-specific |\n| P3 | Expertise depth |\n\n```yaml\npattern: P1\npattern: P2\npattern: P3\n```\n\n### stacking (REQUIRED)\n\n**Type:** integer  \n**Range:** 0-3\n\n```yaml\nstacking: 1   # Counts against stack limit\nstacking: 0   # Does not count (meta skills)\n```\n\n**Note:** hivemind-skill-writer has stacking: 0 because it's a meta skill.\n\n### owner (REQUIRED)\n\n**Type:** string  \n**Value:** `hivemind`\n\n```yaml\nowner: hivemind\n```\n\n### status (REQUIRED)\n\n**Type:** string  \n**Values:** active, deprecated, draft, archived\n\n```yaml\nstatus: active      # Ready for use\nstatus: draft       # In development\nstatus: deprecated  # Will be removed\nstatus: archived    # Historical only\n```\n\n### tags (OPTIONAL)\n\n**Type:** array of strings\n\n```yaml\ntags: [delegation, scope, hierarchy]\ntags: [context, rot, recovery]\n```\n\n### depends-on (OPTIONAL)\n\n**Type:** array of strings\n\n```yaml\ndepends-on:\n  - context-intelligence\n  - delegation-scope\n```\n\n---\n\n## Validation Checklist\n\n- [ ] name is kebab-case\n- [ ] description starts with \"Use when...\"\n- [ ] version is valid semver\n- [ ] framework is \"hivemind\"\n- [ ] pack is recognized\n- [ ] entry-level is L1, L2, or L3\n- [ ] pattern is P1, P2, or P3\n- [ ] stacking is 0-3\n- [ ] owner is \"hivemind\"\n- [ ] status is valid value\n\n---\n\n## Examples\n\n### P1 Entry Skill\n\n```yaml\n---\nname: context-intelligence\ndescription: Use when starting a session, resuming after interruption, detecting context drift, or when delegation scope is unclear. Provides context rot defense and trust scoring.\nversion: 1.0.0\nframework: hivemind\npack: context-intelligence\nentry-level: L1\npattern: P1\nstacking: 1\nowner: hivemind\nstatus: active\n---\n```\n\n### P2 Sub-Pack Skill\n\n```yaml\n---\nname: delegation-scope\ndescription: Use when delegating to subagents or receiving delegated scope. Covers scope inheritance, chain of command, and anti-patterns.\nversion: 1.0.0\nframework: hivemind\npack: context-intelligence/delegation\nentry-level: L2\npattern: P2\nstacking: 1\nowner: hivemind\nstatus: active\ndepends-on:\n  - context-intelligence\n---\n```\n\n### P3 Recovery Skill\n\n```yaml\n---\nname: context-rot-recovery\ndescription: Use when context rot severity exceeds 9. Activated by context-intelligence when degradation is detected beyond safe thresholds.\nversion: 1.0.0\nframework: hivemind\npack: context-intelligence/recovery\nentry-level: L3\npattern: P3\nstacking: 1\nowner: hivemind\nstatus: active\ndepends-on:\n  - context-intelligence\n---\n```\n\n### Meta Skill (No Stack)\n\n```yaml\n---\nname: hivemind-skill-writer\ndescription: Use when creating, auditing, refactoring, or packaging HiveMind framework skills. Activates the meta-builder for skill authoring.\nversion: 1.0.0\nframework: hivemind\npack: hivemind-skill-writer\nentry-level: L1\npattern: P1\nstacking: 0\nowner: hivemind\nstatus: active\n---\n```\n\n---\n\n## Anti-Patterns\n\n**WRONG:**\n```yaml\nname: contextIntelligence      # camelCase\nname: context_intelligence     # snake_case\nname: Context-Intelligence     # PascalCase\n```\n\n**RIGHT:**\n```yaml\nname: context-intelligence     # kebab-case\n```\n\n**WRONG:**\n```yaml\ndescription: Manages context    # Too vague\ndescription: Use always         # Not specific\n```\n\n**RIGHT:**\n```yaml\ndescription: Use when starting a session, resuming after interruption, or detecting context drift. Provides defense against context rot.\n```\n",

{
  "content": "# The 3 Patterns System\n\n## Purpose\n\nDesign patterns for HiveMind skills. Choose the right pattern based on purpose and depth needed.\n\n---\n\n## Overview\n\n| Pattern | Purpose | Depth | Stacking | When to Use |\n|---------|---------|-------|----------|-------------|\n| **P1** | High-level routing | Shallow | 1 | Entry skills, meta skills |\n| **P2** | Domain-specific | Medium | 1 | Sub-pack skills, focused guidance |\n| **P3** | Expertise depth | Deep | 1 | Complex scenarios, recovery |\n\n---\n\n## Pattern 1: High-Level Routing\n\n### Characteristics\n\n- Thin, must-load entry skills\n- Simple routing logic\n- Minimal body (<200 lines)\n- References for detail\n\n### Structure\n\n```markdown\n# Skill Name\n\n## Purpose\nThin routing skill that directs to specialized sub-packs.\n\n## When to Activate\n- Condition A\n- Condition B\n- Condition C\n\n## Routing Logic\nIF [condition A] → load [sub-pack-A]\nIF [condition B] → load [sub-pack-B]\nELSE → load [default]\n\n## References\nSee references/ for detailed guidance.\n```\n\n### Examples\n\n| Skill | Pack | Routing Target |\n|-------|------|---------------|\n| `context-intelligence` | context-intelligence | delegation, workflow, recovery |\n| `hivemind-skill-writer` | hivemind-skill-writer | anatomy, quality, tdd |\n| `explore-context` | explore | deep-scan, surface |\n\n### Stacking with P1\n\n```\nP1 (1) + P2 (1) = 2 skills\nP1 (1) + P2 (1) + P2 (1) = 3 skills\nP1 (1) + P3 (1) = 2 skills\n```\n\n---\n\n## Pattern 2: Domain-Specific\n\n### Characteristics\n\n- Deeper guidance for specific domains\n- Step-by-step process\n- Templates and matrices\n- 200-500 lines\n\n### Structure\n\n```markdown\n# Skill Name\n\n## Purpose\nDomain-specific guidance for [specific area].\n\n## When to Activate\n- Condition A\n- Condition B\n\n## Core Process\n\n### Step 1: [Name]\nDescription of step...\n\n### Step 2: [Name]\nDescription of step...\n\n### Step 3: [Name]\nDescription of step...\n\n## Templates\n- [Template link]\n\n## Anti-Patterns\n- What NOT to do\n- Common mistakes\n- Edge cases to avoid\n\n## References\nDetailed reference material...\n```\n\n### Examples\n\n| Skill | Domain | Steps |\n|-------|--------|-------|\n| `delegation-scope` | Delegation | Declare → Inherit → Verify → Execute |\n| `workflow-hierarchy` | Workflows | Plan → Implement → Verify → Deliver |\n| `skill-anatomy` | Skill Writing | Discover → Design → Implement → Validate |\n\n### Stacking with P2\n\n```\nP1 (1) + P2 (1) = 2 skills\nP2 (1) + P2 (1) = 2 skills\nP1 (1) + P2 (1) + P2 (1) = 3 skills\n```\n\n---\n\n## Pattern 3: Expertise Depth\n\n### Characteristics\n\n- Vertical depth for complex scenarios\n- Heavy reference bundle\n- TOC with jump links\n- >500 lines OR reference-heavy\n\n### Structure\n\n```markdown\n# Skill Name\n\n## Overview\nBrief overview of the expertise area.\n\n## Table of Contents\n- [Section A](#section-a)\n- [Section B](#section-b)\n- [Section C](#section-c)\n\n## Section A\nTarget content for section A...\n\n## Section B\nTarget content for section B...\n\n## Section C\nTarget content for section C...\n\n---\n\n# Reference Bundle\n\n## Detailed Topic A\nHeavy content for A...\n\n## Detailed Topic B\nHeavy content for B...\n\n---\n\n## index.md (Separate File)\n\n# Table of Contents\n\n## Main Sections\n- [Section A](#section-a) — Brief description\n- [Section B](#section-b) — Brief description\n- [Section C](#section-c) — Brief description\n\n## Reference Bundle\n- [Topic A](#detailed-topic-a) — Deep dive\n- [Topic B](#detailed-topic-b) — Deep dive\n\n## Jump Links\nMain file: [SKILL.md](./SKILL.md)\n```\n\n### Examples\n\n| Skill | Scenario | Content |\n|-------|----------|---------|\n| `context-rot-recovery` | Rot > 9 | Emergency protocols |\n| `codebase-deep-scan` | Investigation | Full investigation |\n\n### Stacking with P3\n\n```\nP1 (1) + P3 (1) = 2 skills\nP1 (1) + P2 (1) + P3 (1) = 3 skills\n```\n\n---\n\n## Choosing the Right Pattern\n\n### Decision Tree\n\n```\nIs this an entry/routing skill?\n├── YES → P1\n└── NO\n    ├── Is this a focused domain skill?\n    │   ├── YES → P2\n    │   └── NO\n    │       ├── Is this a complex/expertise skill?\n    │       ├── YES → P3\n    │       └── NO → P2\n```\n\n### When to Use P1\n\n- Entry skills that route to sub-packs\n- Meta skills (like hivemind-skill-writer)\n- Thin skills that just delegate\n\n### When to Use P2\n\n- Sub-pack skills with clear domain focus\n- Step-by-step processes\n- Skills with templates/matrices\n\n### When to Use P3\n\n- Recovery skills\n- Complex investigation skills\n- Skills needing heavy reference bundle\n- Skills where P1/P2 is insufficient\n\n---\n\n## Anti-Patterns\n\n### P1 Anti-Patterns\n\n- **Too thick**: P1 should be <200 lines\n- **Missing routing**: No clear IF-THEN logic\n- **No references**: P1 without references means no depth path\n\n### P2 Anti-Patterns\n\n- **Too shallow**: Should have real depth\n- **Too many steps**: Max 5-7 steps\n- **No templates**: P2 should have practical templates\n\n### P3 Anti-Patterns\n\n- **Unnecessary complexity**: If P1/P2 works, don't use P3\n- **Missing TOC**: P3 MUST have table of contents\n- **Broken jump links**: Verify all links work\n\n---\n\n## Reference Depth Rule\n\n```\nSKILL.md (Entry Point)\n    │\n    ├── L1: Overview + TOC\n    ├── L2: Core sections\n    │\n    └── references/ (1-level deep)\n            ├── 01-topic-a.md\n            ├── 02-topic-b.md\n            └── index.md (TOC for P3)\n\nreferences/ files CANNOT reference other references/\n```\n\n**Exception:** P3 index.md can have jump links to SKILL.md sections.\n",
  "filePath": "/Users/apple/hivemind-plugin/skills/hivemind-skill-writer/references/03-three-patterns.md"
}
```

{
  "content": "# TDD Workflow for Skills\n\n## Purpose\n\nTest-driven development methodology for HiveMind skill authoring. Every skill MUST be validated against real failure scenarios before being written.\n\n---\n\n## The Iron Law\n\n> **NO SKILL WITHOUT A FAILING TEST FIRST**\n\n---\n\n## Overview\n\n```\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│                    TDD CYCLE FOR SKILLS                       │\n├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤\n│                                                              │\n│   ┌─────────┐    ┌─────────┐    ┌─────────────┐            │\n│   │   RED   │ →  │  GREEN  │ →  │  REFACTOR   │            │\n│   │  Phase  │    │  Phase  │    │    Phase    │            │\n│   └─────────┘    └─────────┘    └─────────────┘            │\n│        │              │                │                    │\n│        │              │                │                    │\n│        ▼              ▼                ▼                    │\n│   Identify        Write           Remove                     │\n│   failure         minimal         duplication                │\n│   scenario        skill           Tighten                    │\n│                                   triggers                  │\n│                                                              │\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\n---\n\n## RED Phase: Identify Failure\n\n### Step 1: Capture the Failing Scenario\n\n**Question:** What specific scenario does NOT work without this skill?\n\n**Format:**\n```markdown\n## Failing Scenario: [Name]\n\n### Input\n[What triggers the scenario]\n\n### Expected Behavior\n[What should happen]\n\n### Without Skill\n[What actually happens - THE FAILURE]\n\n### Evidence\n[How to verify this fails]\n```\n\n### Step 2: Write the Test Prompt\n\nCreate a test that would pass WITH the skill but fail WITHOUT it:\n\n```markdown\n## Test Prompt: [Scenario Name]\n\nYou are in a [session state].\n\nYour task: [specific task]\n\nWithout hivemind-skill-writer loaded:\n- [Observed behavior - FAIL]\n\nWith hivemind-skill-writer loaded:\n- [Expected behavior - PASS]\n```\n\n### Step 3: Run Baseline\n\n1. Clear any skill loading\n2. Execute the test prompt\n3. Observe and document the exact failure\n4. Capture evidence (output, errors, behavior)\n\n### Step 4: Document Failure Mode\n\n```markdown\n## Failure Evidence: [Date]\n\n**Observed:** [Exact behavior]\n**Expected:** [What should happen]\n**Gap:** [The difference]\n**Severity:** [Impact level]\n```\n\n---\n\n## GREEN Phase: Write the Skill\n\n### Step 1: Design Minimal Skill\n\nAddress ONLY the failure scenario. Do not add features.\n\n**Checklist:**\n- [ ] Does this address the failing scenario?\n- [ ] Is this the minimum needed?\n- [ ] Does this introduce ceremony?\n- [ ] Does this conflict with existing skills?\n\n### Step 2: Write SKILL.md\n\nFollow the anatomy template and frontmatter standard.\n\n```yaml\n---\nname: skill-name\ndescription: Use when [trigger] — [effect]\nversion: 1.0.0\nframework: hivemind\npack: pack-name\nentry-level: L1|L2|L3\npattern: P1|P2|P3\nstacking: 0-3\nowner: hivemind\nstatus: draft\n---\n```\n\n### Step 3: Create References (if needed)\n\nFor P2/P3, create minimal reference bundle.\n\n### Step 4: Run with Skill\n\n1. Load the skill\n2. Execute the same test prompt\n3. Verify behavior change\n4. Document success criteria\n\n### Step 5: Document Success\n\n```markdown\n## Success Evidence: [Date]\n\n**Before:** [Failure mode]\n**After:** [Fixed behavior]\n**Evidence:** [Verification output]\n```\n\n---\n\n## REFACTOR Phase: Improve\n\n### Step 1: Remove Duplication\n\n- Check for overlap with existing skills\n- Consolidate common patterns\n- Ensure non-redundancy\n\n### Step 2: Tighten Triggers\n\n- Is description specific enough?\n- Any false positive triggers?\n- Any missed triggering conditions?\n\n### Step 3: Validate Structure\n\n- [ ] Reference depth = 1 level\n- [ ] Stacking ≤3\n- [ ] Frontmatter complete\n- [ ] No broken links\n\n### Step 4: Run Skill-Judge\n\nEvaluate against 5 dimensions:\n1. Trigger Accuracy (25%)\n2. Action Coherence (25%)\n3. Reference Integrity (20%)\n4. Non-Redundancy (15%)\n5. Edge Case Coverage (15%)\n\n---\n\n## Scenario Library\n\n### Entry State Scenarios\n\n| Scenario | Description | Pattern |\n|----------|-------------|---------|\n| FRESH_ENTRY | New session without context | P1 |\n| RESUME_GAP | Resume after context prune | P1 |\n| DELEGATE_AMBIGUITY | Unclear delegation scope | P2 |\n| ROT_DETECTED | Context drift detected | P3 |\n\n### Quality Scenarios\n\n| Scenario | Description | Pattern |\n|----------|-------------|---------|\n| TRIGGER_VAGUE | Description too broad | Refactor |\n| STACK_OVERFLOW | >3 skills at entry | Refactor |\n| REF_DEPTH_2 | 2-level references | Refactor |\n\n### Non-Breaking Scenarios\n\n| Scenario | Description | Expected |\n|----------|-------------|----------|\n| GSD_AFFECTED | GSD workflows still work | Unaffected |\n| NO_CEREMONY | No added workflow friction | No overhead |\n| STACK_OK | 3 skills max | Compliant |\n\n---\n\n## Test Templates\n\n### Template 1: Entry Scenario Test\n\n```markdown\n## Test: [Scenario Name]\n\n**Given:** [Preconditions]\n**When:** [Action taken]\n**Then:** [Expected result]\n\n**Without Skill:**\n```\n[Observed output]\n```\n\n**With Skill:**\n```\n[Expected output]\n```\n\n**PASS/FAIL:** [Result]\n```\n\n### Template 2: Non-Breaking Test\n\n```markdown\n## Test: GSD Compatibility\n\n**Given:** GSD workflow execution\n**When:** Skill is loaded\n**Then:** GSD workflow completes normally\n\n**Result:** PASS/FAIL\n```\n\n### Template 3: Quality Test\n\n```markdown\n## Test: Skill-Judge Evaluation\n\n**Skill:** [Name]\n**Dimensions:**\n- Trigger Accuracy: [1-5]\n- Action Coherence: [1-5]\n- Reference Integrity: [1-5]\n- Non-Redundancy: [1-5]\n- Edge Case Coverage: [1-5]\n\n**Overall:** [Score]\n**Grade:** [EXCELLENT/GOOD/ACCEPTABLE/NEEDS WORK]\n```\n\n---\n\n## Validation Protocol\n\n### Pre-Commit Checklist\n\n- [ ] RED phase documented\n- [ ] GREEN phase passes\n- [ ] Failure evidence captured\n- [ ] Success evidence captured\n- [ ] Skill-Judge score ≥3.5\n- [ ] No GSD impact\n- [ ] Stacking compliant\n- [ ] Reference depth 1-level\n\n### Skill-Judge Thresholds\n\n| Grade | Action |\n|-------|--------|\n| EXCELLENT (4.5+) | Ready for release |\n| GOOD (4.0+) | Minor polish |\n| ACCEPTABLE (3.0+) | Address gaps |\n| NEEDS WORK (<3.0) | Major revision |\n\n---\n\n## Common Failure Modes\n\n### Mode 1: No Real Failure\n\n**Problem:** Writing skill without identifying actual failure.\n\n**Fix:** Return to RED phase. Identify concrete scenario.\n\n### Mode 2: Scope Creep\n\n**Problem:** Skill does too much.\n\n**Fix:** Focus on minimum viable. Split if needed.\n\n### Mode 3: Vague Trigger\n\n**Problem:** Description too broad/narrow.\n\n**Fix:** Tighten with specific conditions.\n\n### Mode 4: Ceremony Added\n\n**Problem:** Skill adds workflow friction.\n\n**Fix:** Remove mandatory steps. Make optional.\n",
  "filePath": "/Users/apple/hivemind-plugin/skills/hivemind-skill-writer/references/04-tdd-workflow.md"
}

{
  "content": "# Skill Quality Matrix\n\n## Purpose\n\nSkill-Judge evaluation framework for assessing HiveMind skill quality across 5 dimensions.\n\n---\n\n## Evaluation Overview\n\n| Dimension | Weight | Description |\n|-----------|--------|-------------|\n| **Trigger Accuracy** | 25% | Description triggers on specific conditions |\n| **Action Coherence** | 25% | ONE thing well, no mission creep |\n| **Reference Integrity** | 20% | 1-level depth, no circular refs |\n| **Non-Redundancy** | 15% | No overlap with existing skills |\n| **Edge Case Coverage** | 15% | Handles degraded/delegated states |\n\n---\n\n## Scoring Scale\n\n| Score | Rating | Definition |\n|-------|--------|------------|\n| **5** | Excellent | Consistently exceeds expectations |\n| **4** | Good | Meets expectations with minor gaps |\n| **3** | Acceptable | Meets minimum requirements |\n| **2** | Needs Work | Significant gaps |\n| **1** | Poor | Fails minimum requirements |\n\n---\n\n## Dimension 1: Trigger Accuracy (25%)\n\n### What It Measures\n\n- Does the description trigger on specific conditions?\n- Are false positives minimized?\n- Is the trigger unambiguous?\n\n### Evaluation Criteria\n\n| Score | Criteria |\n|-------|----------|\n| **5** | Triggers ONLY on specific conditions, no false positives |\n| **4** | Specific triggers, minimal false positives |\n| **3** | Captures most triggering conditions |\n| **2** | Vague or triggers too broadly |\n| **1** | Generic or non-triggering |\n\n### Good Examples\n\n```yaml\n# Excellent\ndescription: >\n  Use when delegation scope is ambiguous,\n  when inheriting tasks from subagent,\n  or when scope boundaries are unclear.\n\n# Poor\ndescription: >\n  Use when delegating tasks.\n  (Too vague)\n```\n\n### Checklist\n\n- [ ] Description starts with \"Use when...\"\n- [ ] Specific triggering conditions listed\n- [ ] No generic trigger words\n- [ ] False positives minimized\n- [ ] Clear cause-effect stated\n\n---\n\n## Dimension 2: Action Coherence (25%)\n\n### What It Measures\n\n- Does the skill do ONE thing well?\n- Are entry/exit states clear?\n- Is there mission creep?\n\n### Evaluation Criteria\n\n| Score | Criteria |\n|-------|----------|\n| **5** | Single purpose, clear entry/exit, zero mission creep |\n| **4** | Single purpose, minor optional extensions |\n| **3** | Clear primary purpose, some optional scope |\n| **2** | Multiple purposes, unclear boundaries |\n| **1** | Does everything, completely unfocused |\n\n### Good Examples\n\n```markdown\n# Excellent - Single purpose\n## Purpose\nContext rot detection and trust scoring.\nDoes one thing: defends against context degradation.\n\n# Poor - Multiple purposes\n## Purpose\nContext rot detection, delegation management,\nworkflow coordination, AND verification.\n(Too much)\n```\n\n### Checklist\n\n- [ ] Single clear purpose stated\n- [ ] Entry state defined\n- [ ] Exit state defined\n- [ ] No mission creep in body\n- [ ] Boundaries explicitly marked\n\n---\n\n## Dimension 3: Reference Integrity (20%)\n\n### What It Measures\n\n- Is reference depth = 1 level?\n- Are references numbered and ordered?\n- Is TOC present for P3?\n- Are there circular references?\n\n### Evaluation Criteria\n\n| Score | Criteria |\n|-------|----------|\n| **5** | Perfect 1-level depth, logical ordering, clear TOC |\n| **4** | 1-level depth, minor ordering issues |\n| **3** | Some refs could be consolidated |\n| **2** | 2-level depth or circular refs |\n| **1** | Chaotic reference structure |\n\n### Good Structure\n\n```\nskill/\n├── SKILL.md\n└── references/\n    ├── 01-topic-alpha.md      # ✓ Numbered\n    ├── 02-topic-beta.md        # ✓ Numbered\n    └── index.md                # ✓ TOC for P3\n\nreferences/01-topic-alpha.md\n# (No references to other reference files) ✓\n```\n\n### Bad Structure\n\n```\nskill/\n├── SKILL.md\n└── references/\n    ├── 01-topic-alpha.md\n    │   └── references/\n    │       └── nested.md      # ✗ 2-level deep\n    └── 02-topic-beta.md\n        └── \"See 01-topic-alpha.md\"  # ✗ Circular\n```\n\n### Checklist\n\n- [ ] Reference depth = 1 level max\n- [ ] Files numbered for ordering\n- [ ] P3 has index.md with TOC\n- [ ] Jump links functional\n- [ ] No circular references\n\n---\n\n## Dimension 4: Non-Redundancy (15%)\n\n### What It Measures\n\n- Does this overlap with existing skills?\n- Is the purpose distinct?\n- Can boundaries be clearly drawn?\n\n### Evaluation Criteria\n\n| Score | Criteria |\n|-------|----------|\n| **5** | Unique purpose, no overlap |\n| **4** | Minimal overlap, clear boundaries |\n| **3** | Some overlap, but distinct enough |\n| **2** | Significant overlap |\n| **1** | Duplicate of existing skill |\n\n### Cross-Reference Matrix\n\n| Skill | vs context-intelligence | vs delegation-scope | vs workflow-hierarchy |\n|-------|----------------------|-------------------|---------------------|\n| context-intelligence | - | Border | Border |\n| delegation-scope | Border | - | No overlap |\n| workflow-hierarchy | Border | No overlap | - |\n| context-rot-recovery | Extends | No overlap | No overlap |\n\n### Checklist\n\n- [ ] No duplicate of existing skill\n- [ ] Distinct purpose from similar skills\n- [ ] Boundaries clear\n- [ ] Can explain difference in one sentence\n\n---\n\n## Dimension 5: Edge Case Coverage (15%)\n\n### What It Measures\n\n- Does it handle degraded states?\n- Does it handle delegation edge cases?\n- Does it handle post-cancel scenarios?\n- Does it handle late-session drift?\n\n### Entry State Coverage Matrix\n\n| Skill | FRESH | RESUMED | DELEGATED | DEGRADED | POST-CANCEL | LATE |\n|-------|-------|---------|-----------|----------|-------------|------|\n| context-intelligence | ✓ | ✓ | ✓ | ✓ | ✓ | ✓ |\n| delegation-scope | - | ✓ | ✓ | ✓ | ✓ | - |\n| workflow-hierarchy | ✓ | ✓ | - | - | - | ✓ |\n| context-rot-recovery | - | ✓ | - | ✓ | ✓ | ✓ |\n\n### Evaluation Criteria\n\n| Score | Criteria |\n|-------|----------|\n| **5** | All 6 entry states covered, handles complex edges |\n| **4** | Most entry states, common edges handled |\n| **3** | Basic states, some edge handling |\n| **2** | Only basic states, no edge handling |\n| **1** | Doesn't account for session complexity |\n\n### Checklist\n\n- [ ] Entry state recognition present\n- [ ] Degraded state handling\n- [ ] Delegation edge cases\n- [ ] Post-cancel awareness\n- [ ] Late-session drift handling\n\n---\n\n## Overall Score Calculation\n\n### Formula\n\n```\nOverall = (Trigger × 0.25) + \n          (Action × 0.25) + \n          (Reference × 0.20) + \n          (Redundancy × 0.15) + \n          (Edge × 0.15)\n```\n\n### Example Calculation\n\n```\nTrigger:      4 × 0.25 = 1.00\nAction:       5 × 0.25 = 1.25\nReference:    4 × 0.20 = 0.80\nRedundancy:   5 × 0.15 = 0.75\nEdge:         4 × 0.15 = 0.60\n─────────────────────────────\nOverall:                 4.40 = GOOD\n```\n\n### Grade Thresholds\n\n| Overall | Grade | Action |\n|---------|-------|--------|\n| 4.5+ | EXCELLENT | Ready for release |\n| 4.0+ | GOOD | Minor polish |\n| 3.0+ | ACCEPTABLE | Address gaps |\n| <3.0 | NEEDS WORK | Major revision |\n\n---\n\n## Evaluation Template\n\n```markdown\n## Skill-Judge Evaluation: [Skill Name]\n\n**Date:** [YYYY-MM-DD]\n**Evaluator:** [Name/Agent]\n\n### Dimension Scores\n\n| Dimension | Score | Evidence |\n|-----------|-------|----------|\n| Trigger Accuracy | /5 | [Notes] |\n| Action Coherence | /5 | [Notes] |\n| Reference Integrity | /5 | [Notes] |\n| Non-Redundancy | /5 | [Notes] |\n| Edge Case Coverage | /5 | [Notes] |\n\n### Weighted Calculation\n\n```\nTrigger:      [X] × 0.25 = [X.XX]\nAction:       [X] × 0.25 = [X.XX]\nReference:    [X] × 0.20 = [X.XX]\nRedundancy:   [X] × 0.15 = [X.XX]\nEdge:         [X] × 0.15 = [X.XX]\n─────────────────────────────\nOverall:                 [X.XX]\n```\n\n### Grade: [EXCELLENT/GOOD/ACCEPTABLE/NEEDS WORK]\n\n### Strengths\n- [List strengths]\n\n### Weaknesses\n- [List weaknesses]\n\n### Recommendations\n- [List improvements]\n```\n\n---\n\n## Release Criteria\n\n| Criterion | Threshold |\n|-----------|-----------|\n| Overall Score | ≥3.5 |\n| Trigger Accuracy | ≥3.0 |\n| Action Coherence | ≥4.0 |\n| Reference Integrity | ≥3.0 |\n| Non-Redundancy | ≥3.0 |\n| Edge Case Coverage | ≥3.0 |\n\n**All thresholds must be met for release.**\n",
  "filePath": "/Users/apple/hivemind-plugin/skills/hivemind-skill-writer/references/05-skill-quality-matrix.md"
}
```

## Assistant (Build · MiniMax-M2.7 · 16.6s)

_Thinking:_

Now let me create the index.md file for the references directory:

**Tool: write**

**Input:**

{
  "content": "---\nname: context-intelligence\ndescription: Use when starting a session, resuming after interruption, detecting context drift, or when delegation scope is unclear. Provides context rot defense, trust scoring, entry state recognition, and hierarchy awareness. Activates sub-packs based on session state.\nversion: 1.0.0\nframework: hivemind\npack: context-intelligence\nentry-level: L1\npattern: P1\nstacking: 1\nowner: hivemind\nstatus: active\n---\n\n# context-intelligence\n\n## Purpose\n\nAlways-activated defense against context rot, pollution, and poisoning. Routes to specialized sub-packs based on session state.\n\n## When to Activate\n\n**L1 (Always):** On every session start, resume, or continuation\n\n**Secondary Triggers:**\n- Detecting context drift\n- Delegation scope unclear\n- Session state inconsistent\n- After compaction\n- Post-cancel recovery\n\n## Entry State Recognition\n\n| State | Indicators | Required Action |\n|-------|------------|-----------------|\n| **FRESH** | First message, no prior context | Full context map |\n| **RESUMED** | Mid-session continuation, gap possible | Verify prior state |\n| **DELEGATED** | Subagent context, inherited scope | Verify scope |\n| **DEGRADED** | Pruned context, inconsistencies | Assess damage |\n| **POST-CANCEL** | Partial state, interrupted turn | Clean recovery |\n| **LATE-SESSION** | Extended session, accumulated drift | Checkpoint awareness |\n\n## Context Rot Defense\n\n### Detection Signals\n\nIf ANY appear, ASSESS before proceeding:\n\n- Document timestamps contradict git history\n- Governance files reference non-existent entities\n- Skills load unexpectedly or contradict\n- Session state doesn't match observable reality\n- Authority claims conflict at same level\n- Tests pass but implementation is broken\n\n### Severity Taxonomy\n\n| Level | Name | Score | Response |\n|-------|------|-------|----------|\n| **0** | CLEAN | 0-4 | Continue normal ops |\n| **1** | SUSPECT | 5-8 | Verify before critical actions |\n| **2** | DEGRADED | 9-12 | Pause, assess, recover |\n| **3** | POLLUTED | 13-18 | Stop, isolate, rebuild |\n| **4** | POISONED | >18 | Emergency stop, alert user |\n\n### Recovery Protocols\n\n| Severity | Protocol | Action |\n|----------|----------|--------|\n| 0-4 | Continue | Normal operations |\n| 5-8 | Corroborate | Trust canonical surfaces only |\n| 9-12 | Pause | Verify before mutation |\n| 13-18 | Recover | Isolate → Rebuild → Verify |\n\n## Trust Scoring\n\n### Signal Weight Matrix\n\n| Signal | Trust Score | Weight |\n|--------|-------------|--------|\n| Live SDK/plugin behavior | 100% | 1.0 |\n| User confirmation | 100% | 1.0 |\n| Git-verified file | 95% | 0.9 |\n| Type-checked code | 90% | 0.8 |\n| Documentation | 50% | 0.5 |\n| Inherited context | 40% | 0.4 |\n| Unverified claims | 10% | 0.1 |\n\n### Formula\n\n```\nEffective Trust = Σ(Signal × Weight) / Σ(Weight)\n```\n\n**Threshold:** If Effective Trust < 0.6 → Context Rot suspected\n\n## Routing Logic\n\n```\nIF entry state = FRESH\n    → Provide context map\n    → Identify authoritative surfaces\n\nIF entry state = RESUMED\n    → Verify prior state continuity\n    → Check for context pruning\n\nIF entry state = DELEGATED\n    → Load delegation-scope (sub-pack)\n    → Verify scope inheritance\n\nIF rot severity > 9\n    → Load context-rot-recovery (sub-pack)\n    → Initiate recovery protocol\n\nIF workflow invoked\n    → Load workflow-hierarchy (sub-pack)\n    → Coordinate planning → implementation → verification\n```\n\n## Hierarchy Rules\n\n1. **Source Authority** > **Project Authority** > **Inherited Authority**\n2. **Latest Valid Same-Level Authority** when logically justified\n3. **Own Scope** > **Inherited Scope** — always know boundary\n4. **Pattern Matching** > **Hardcoded Paths** — prefer regex where safe\n\n## High-Impact Action Gates\n\n| Action | Trust Required | Confirmation |\n|--------|---------------|--------------|\n| Read files | 0.4 | None |\n| Write files | 0.6 | User if < 0.7 |\n| Delete files | 0.8 | Always confirm |\n| Execute commands | 0.7 | User if < 0.8 |\n| Delegate | 0.6 | Explicit scope |\n| Claim completion | 0.8 | Evidence required |\n\n## Anti-Patterns\n\n**DO NOT:**\n- Trust inherited context without verification\n- Assume same-level authority is current\n- Ignore timestamp inconsistencies\n- Proceed when trust < 0.6\n- Delegate without explicit scope declaration\n- Claim completion without evidence\n\n**DO:**\n- Verify before critical actions\n- Score trust using the matrix\n- Acknowledge entry state\n- Route to sub-packs when triggered\n- Maintain hierarchy awareness\n- Document rot evidence\n\n## Sub-Packs\n\n| Sub-Pack | Trigger | Purpose |\n|----------|---------|---------|\n| `delegation-scope` | Delegation intent | Scope inheritance, chain of command |\n| `workflow-hierarchy` | Workflow invoke | Planning → Implementation → Verification |\n| `context-rot-recovery` | Rot severity >9 | Emergency recovery protocols |\n\n## References\n\n- `references/01-context-rot-taxonomy.md` — Severity levels 0-4\n- `references/02-entry-state-matrix.md` — Session state details\n- `references/03-trust-matrix.md` — Trust scoring system\n- `references/04-delegation-scope-rules.md` — Scope inheritance\n- `references/05-platform-surface-matrix.md` — Cross-platform awareness\n",
  "filePath": "/Users/apple/hivemind-plugin/skills/context-intelligence/SKILL.md"

  "content": "# Context Rot Taxonomy\n\n## Severity Levels\n\n### Level 0: CLEAN\n\nAll context signals are consistent with authoritative sources.\n\n**Indicators:**\n- All file references resolve\n- Governance documents align\n- Timestamps consistent with git\n- Delegation chains are traceable\n\n**Response:** Continue normal operations\n\n**Score Range:** 0-4\n\n---\n\n### Level 1: SUSPECT\n\nMinor inconsistencies that don't affect core functionality.\n\n**Indicators:**\n- 1-2 minor timestamp mismatches\n- Single document reference could be stale\n- Minor cosmetic inconsistencies\n\n**Response:** Note and verify before critical actions\n\n**Score Range:** 5-8\n\n---\n\n### Level 2: DEGRADED\n\nSignificant context drift affecting workflow coherence.\n\n**Indicators:**\n- Multiple timestamp conflicts\n- Some referenced files don't exist\n- Delegation scope unclear\n- Test assertions don't match code\n- Gap in session history\n\n**Response:** Pause, perform full context assessment, recover\n\n**Score Range:** 9-12\n\n---\n\n### Level 3: POLLUTED\n\nMajor conflicts that break trust in context integrity.\n\n**Indicators:**\n- Conflicting authority claims at same level\n- Governance references non-existent entities\n- Skill triggers contradict each other\n- Significant gap in session state\n- Tests pass but implementation clearly broken\n\n**Response:** Stop execution, isolate polluted context, rebuild from authoritative sources\n\n**Score Range:** 13-18\n\n---\n\n### Level 4: POISONED\n\nDangerous or potentially malicious context injection.\n\n**Indicators:**\n- Authority claims that are demonstrably false\n- Test assertions that pass but encode wrong behavior\n- Governance that would cause harmful actions\n- Manipulated git history signals\n- Deliberate misdirection in artifacts\n\n**Response:** EMERGENCY STOP. Alert user immediately. Await explicit instruction.\n\n**Score Range:** >18\n\n---\n\n## Detection Dimensions\n\n### D1: Governance Integrity\n\n- [ ] All referenced files exist\n- [ ] AGENTS.md references current\n- [ ] Skill triggers match content\n- [ ] Authority signals are legitimate\n\n### D2: Temporal Consistency\n\n- [ ] Timestamps align with git history\n- [ ] Recent changes in context\n- [ ] No future-dated artifacts\n- [ ] Same-level authority resolved logically\n\n### D3: Delegation Scope\n\n- [ ] Chain traceable\n- [ ] Boundaries explicit\n- [ ] No scope creep\n- [ ] Parent-child clear\n\n### D4: Workflow Integrity\n\n- [ ] P→I→V→D flow intact\n- [ ] No orphaned artifacts\n- [ ] Tests match implementation\n- [ ] Handoffs clean\n\n### D5: Platform Surface\n\n- [ ] Paths correct for platform\n- [ ] Cross-platform awareness accurate\n- [ ] No phantom references\n- [ ] Symlinks resolve\n\n---\n\n## Scoring Rubric\n\n| Dimension | Weight | Score 0 | Score 1 | Score 2 | Score 3 |\n|-----------|--------|---------|---------|---------|---------|\n| **Authority Ambiguity** | High | No ambiguity | Minor | Significant | Major conflict |\n| **Deterministic Enforcement** | High | None | Minor | Significant | Blocking |\n| **Load-Path Pressure** | Medium | None | Minor | Significant | Hijacking |\n| **Action Enablement** | High | None | Minor | Significant | Harmful |\n| **Propagation Breadth** | Medium | None | 1 layer | 2-3 layers | Deep |\n| **Freshness/Drift** | Medium | Current | Minor drift | Significant | Stale |\n\n**Score each dimension 0-3, sum for total (0-18)**\n\n---\n\n## Recovery Protocols\n\n### Protocol Alpha: Self-Recovery\n\nFor Level 1-2\n\n1. Isolate suspicious context\n2. Rebuild from nearest clean source\n3. Cross-verify with git history\n4. Continue if trust > 0.7\n\n### Protocol Beta: User-Assisted\n\nFor Level 2-3\n\n1. Stop execution\n2. Present evidence of rot\n3. Request user confirmation\n4. Follow user guidance\n\n### Protocol Gamma: Emergency\n\nFor Level 3-4\n\n1. Halt all actions\n2. Alert user with evidence\n3. Await explicit instruction\n4. Document incident\n",

Map project context\n2. Identify authoritative surfaces\n3. Note any pre-existing state\n4. Establish baseline trust score\n\n**Sub-Pack Activation:** None by default\n\n---\n\n### RESUMED SESSION\n\n**Definition:** Continuation after natural context window\n\n**Indicators:**\n- Prior context exists but may be pruned\n- Gap in conversation history\n- Session ID continues\n\n**Required Actions:**\n1. Verify prior state markers\n2. Check for gaps in trajectory\n3. Re-establish continuity\n4. Assess context completeness\n\n**Sub-Pack Activation:** `context-rot-recovery` if drift detected\n\n---\n\n### DELEGATED SESSION\n\n**Definition:** Subagent or child session with inherited scope\n\n**Indicators:**\n- Received delegated task\n- Explicit scope declaration present\n- Working within boundaries\n\n**Required Actions:**\n1. Understand inherited vs. own scope\n2. Verify delegation chain\n3. Do NOT inherit parent session state\n4. Stay within declared boundaries\n\n**Sub-Pack Activation:** `delegation-scope` (auto)\n\n---\n\n### DEGRADED SESSION\n\n**Definition:** State where context integrity is compromised\n\n**Indicators:**\n- Pruned context window\n- Missing mid-session artifacts\n- Unclear what preceded current state\n- Contradictory signals\n\n**Required Actions:**\n1. STOP assuming prior state is accurate\n2. Rebuild context from authoritative sources\n3. Verify key facts independently\n4. Score trust level\n\n**Sub-Pack Activation:** `context-rot-recovery` (auto)\n\n---\n\n### INTERRUPTED SESSION\n\n**Definition:** Resumed after cancellation or error\n\n**Indicators:**\n- Prior action was incomplete\n- No clear outcome from previous turn\n- State may be partially written\n\n**Required Actions:**\n1. Assess what completed vs. what didn't\n2. Verify state integrity\n3. Resume or restart as appropriate\n4. Document any ambiguity\n\n**Sub-Pack Activation:** `context-rot-recovery` if severity >9\n\n---\n\n### RECOVERED SESSION\n\n**Definition:** After successful context repair\n\n**Indicators:**\n- Context integrity restored\n- Trust score returned to normal\n- Prior issues documented\n\n**Required Actions:**\n1. Verify restoration\n2. Continue with confidence\n3. Document recovery path\n\n**Sub-Pack Activation:** None\n\n---\n\n## State Transition Matrix\n\n```\nNEW ──────────────────────────────────────────────► RESUMED\n  │                                                    │\n  │ (context prune, gap, continued work)               │\n  ▼                                                    ▼\nDEGRADED ◄────────────────────────────────────── INTERRUPTED\n  │                                                    │\n  │ (resolve)                                          │ (resolve)\n  ▼                                                    ▼\nRECOVERED ─────────────────────────────────────────► RESUMED\n\nDELEGATED ────────────────────────────────────────► (work)\n     │                                                    │\n     │ (complete)                                        │\n     ▼                                                    ▼\n  RESUMED ◄──────────────────────────────────────► DELEGATED\n```\n\n---\n\n## Entry State Recognition Checklist\n\nWhen starting any session:\n\n- [ ] Identify current state (FRESH/RESUMED/DELEGATED/DEGRADED/INTERRUPTED)\n- [ ] Check for prior context markers\n- [ ] Verify session continuity\n- [ ] Assess trust level\n- [ ] Activate sub-packs as needed\n\n---\n\n## State-Specific Trust Thresholds\n\n| State | Minimum Trust | Action if Below |\n|-------|--------------|-----------------|\n| NEW | 0.6 | Full context map |\n| RESUMED | 0.5 | Verify continuity |\n| DELEGATED | 0.6 | Verify scope |\n| DEGRADED | 0.7 | Recover first |\n| INTERRUPTED | 0.5 | Assess integrity |\n| RECOVERED | 0.6 | Verify restoration |\n",

  "content": "# Trust Matrix\n\n## Trust Scoring System\n\nQuantifies reliability of context signals for decision-making.\n\n---\n\n## Signal Weight Matrix\n\n| Signal | Trust Score | Weight | Notes |\n|--------|-------------|--------|-------|\n| Live SDK/plugin behavior | 100% | 1.0 | Direct API |\n| User confirmation | 100% | 1.0 | Direct input |\n| Git-verified file | 95% | 0.9 | Version controlled |\n| Type-checked code | 90% | 0.8 | Compiler verified |\n| Documentation | 50% | 0.5 | May be stale |\n| Inherited context | 40% | 0.4 | Second-hand |\n| Unverified claims | 10% | 0.1 | Hearsay |\n| Contradictory signals | 0% | 0.0 | Cancel out |\n\n---\n\n## Calculation Formula\n\n```\nEffective Trust = Σ(Signal × Weight) / Σ(Weight)\n```\n\n### Example 1: Clean Session\n\n```\nGit-verified file:     0.95 × 0.9 = 0.855\nType-checked code:     0.90 × 0.8 = 0.720\nUser confirmation:      1.00 × 1.0 = 1.000\nDocumentation:         0.50 × 0.5 = 0.250\n────────────────────────────────────────\nSum:                   Σ(Weight) = 3.2\nTrust:                 2.825 / 3.2 = 0.883 ≈ 88%\n```\n\n### Example 2: Degraded Session\n\n```\nGit-verified file:     0.95 × 0.9 = 0.855\nDocumentation:         0.50 × 0.5 = 0.250\nInherited context:     0.40 × 0.4 = 0.160\nUnverified claims:     0.10 × 0.1 = 0.010\n────────────────────────────────────────\nSum:                   Σ(Weight) = 1.9\nTrust:                 1.275 / 1.9 = 0.671 ≈ 67%\n```\n\n---\n\n## Trust Thresholds\n\n| Threshold | Level | Behavior |\n|-----------|-------|----------|\n| **≥0.8** | HIGH | Full confidence |\n| **0.6-0.79** | MEDIUM | Verify before critical |\n| **0.4-0.59** | LOW | Trust canonical only |\n| **<0.4** | CRITICAL | Recover context |\n\n---\n\n## Action Thresholds\n\n### Default Thresholds\n\n| Action | Minimum Trust | Confirmation |\n|--------|--------------|--------------|\n| Read files | 0.4 | None |\n| Write files | 0.6 | User if < 0.7 |\n| Delete files | 0.8 | Always confirm |\n| Execute commands | 0.7 | User if < 0.8 |\n| Delegate | 0.6 | Explicit scope |\n| Claim completion | 0.8 | Evidence required |\n\n### State-Specific Adjustments\n\n| State | Default Modifier | Rationale |\n|-------|-----------------|-----------|\n| NEW | +0.1 | Building from scratch |\n| RESUMED | 0 | Baseline |\n| DELEGATED | +0.1 | Extra verification |\n| DEGRADED | +0.2 | Requires trust restoration |\n| INTERRUPTED | +0.1 | State uncertain |\n| LATE-SESSION | +0.15 | Accumulated drift |\n\n---\n\n## Trust Signal Checklist\n\nWhen assessing trust:\n\n- [ ] Identify all signals present\n- [ ] Score each signal (0-1)\n- [ ] Apply weights\n- [ ] Calculate effective trust\n- [ ] Compare to threshold\n- [ ] Determine action\n\n---\n\n## Trust Recovery\n\nIf trust falls below threshold:\n\n1. **Isolate** suspicious context\n2. **Identify** reliable signals\n3. **Rebuild** from authoritative sources\n4. **Verify** with user confirmation\n5. **Document** recovery path\n\n---\n\n## Anti-Patterns\n\n**DO NOT:**\n- Mix signals of different reliability\n- Weight unverified claims equally with verified\n- Ignore contradictory signals\n- Proceed below minimum threshold\n- Skip verification when trust is medium\n\n**DO:**\n- Separate signal categories\n- Weight by reliability\n- Detect contradictions\n- Respect thresholds\n- Verify when uncertain\n",

{
  "content": "# Delegation Scope Rules\n\n## Scope Inheritance Matrix\n\n| Element | Inherit? | Rationale |\n|---------|----------|-----------|\n| Task description | YES | Core mandate |\n| Constraints | YES | Operating bounds |\n| Success criteria | YES | Target definition |\n| Parent session state | NO | Privacy, isolation |\n| Unrelated context | NO | Scope containment |\n| Authority to delegate further | NO | Chain of command |\n| Parent's internal doubts | NO | Noise reduction |\n\n---\n\n## Scope Declaration Protocol\n\n### When Receiving Delegation\n\n```\nSCOPE DECLARATION:\n- Task: [specific task]\n- Constraints: [bounds]\n- Success: [measurable outcome]\n- Duration: [expected scope lifetime]\n- Boundaries: [what is NOT in scope]\n```\n\n### When Granting Delegation\n\n```\nSCOPE GRANT:\n- Agent: [subagent identifier]\n- Task: [specific task]\n- Constraints: [bounds + authority level]\n- Success: [measurable outcome]\n- Reporting: [how to report back]\n```\n\n---\n\n## Chain of Command\n\n### Authority Levels\n\n1. **ORIGINAL AUTHORITY** — User or top-level agent\n2. **PRIMARY DELEGATOR** — First-level delegate with full context\n3. **SUBAGENT** — Limited scope, task-specific\n\n### Rule\n\nEach level can only delegate what it received + its own level additions.\n\n```\nUser (Original Authority)\n    │\n    └──► hiveminder (Primary Delegator)\n              │\n              └──► hivemaker (Subagent)\n                        │\n                        └──► hivemaker can ONLY:\n                             - Work within granted scope\n                             - Report to hiveminder\n                             - NOT further delegate\n```\n\n---\n\n## Anti-Patterns\n\n### Scope Bleed\n\n**Problem:** Parent context leaking into subagent\n\n**Indicators:**\n- Subagent acting on parent's unrelated tasks\n- Unclear boundaries causing mixed outputs\n- Results contaminated by parent context\n\n**Fix:** Explicit scope declaration, verify boundaries\n\n### Scope Creep\n\n**Problem:** Subagent taking initiative beyond granted scope\n\n**Indicators:**\n- Adding tasks not in original delegation\n- Extending duration beyond specified\n- Making decisions outside scope\n\n**Fix:** Reference scope declaration, ask before expanding\n\n### Scope Abandonment\n\n**Problem:** Subagent ignoring constraints\n\n**Indicators:**\n- Acting without reporting\n- Abandoning task mid-execution\n- Ignoring stated boundaries\n\n**Fix:** Re-establish scope, verify compliance\n\n---\n\n## Verification Checklist\n\nFor every delegation:\n\n- [ ] Scope declared explicitly\n- [ ] Boundaries stated clearly\n- [ ] Success criteria measurable\n- [ ] Reporting method defined\n- [ ] Duration reasonable\n\n---\n\n## Subagent Checklist\n\nWhen working as subagent:\n\n- [ ] Understand inherited vs. own scope\n- [ ] Verify delegation chain\n- [ ] Do NOT inherit parent session state\n- [ ] Stay within declared boundaries\n- [ ] Report at specified points\n- [ ] Ask before scope expansion\n",
  "filePath": "/Users/apple/hivemind-plugin/skills/context-intelligence/references/04-delegation-scope-rules.md"
}

  "content": "# Platform Surface Matrix\n\n## Multi-Platform Awareness\n\nHiveMind operates in multi-platform environments. Skills must handle platform differences.\n\n---\n\n## Platform Detection\n\n### Entry Surfaces\n\n| Platform | Directory | Agent Pattern |\n|----------|-----------|---------------|\n| OpenCode | `.opencode/` | `gsd-*` |\n| Claude Code | `.claude/` | `claude-*` |\n| Codex | `.codex/` | `codex-*` |\n| Cursor | `.cursor/` | `cursor-*` |\n| Gemini | `.gemini/` | `gemini-*` |\n\n### Discovery Pattern\n\n```bash\n# Safe discovery (read-only)\nls -la | grep -E '^\\.' | grep -v '^\\.\\.$|^\\.$'\n\n# Cross-platform skill discovery\nfind . -maxdepth 2 -type d -name 'skills' 2>/dev/null\n```\n\n---\n\n## Cross-Platform Skill Paths\n\n| Surface | Platform | Type |\n|---------|----------|------|\n| `skills/` | Project | Native HiveMind |\n| `.opencode/skills/` | OpenCode | Runtime projection |\n| `.claude/skills/` | Claude Code | Local |\n| `.codex/skills/` | Codex | Local |\n| `.github/skills/` | External | Reference |\n\n---\n\n## Path Handling Rules\n\n### Safe Patterns\n\n```bash\n# Use relative paths where possible\n# Prefer pattern matching over absolute paths\n\n# GOOD\n./src/**/*.ts\n**/skills/*/SKILL.md\n\n# AVOID\n/home/user/project/src/file.ts\n/Users/apple/hivemind-plugin/src\n```\n\n### Cross-Platform Commands\n\n| Task | Linux/macOS | Windows |\n|------|-------------|---------|\n| List files | `ls -la` | `dir /a` |\n| Find pattern | `grep -r` | `Get-ChildItem -Recurse` |\n| Path separator | `/` | `\\` |\n\n---\n\n## Platform-Specific Considerations\n\n### OpenCode (Primary)\n\n- Skills load from `skills/` and `.opencode/skills/`\n- Agent discovery in `.opencode/agents/`\n- Commands in `.opencode/commands/`\n\n### Claude Code\n\n- Skills in `.claude/skills/`\n- Uses `CLAUDE.md` for project rules\n- Different context window behavior\n\n### Others\n\n- Each platform has different conventions\n- Detect platform before applying rules\n- Use generic patterns where possible\n\n---\n\n## Symlink Handling\n\n### Discovery\n\n```bash\n# Find broken symlinks\nfind . -type l ! -exec test -e {} \\; -print 2>/dev/null\n\n# Find valid symlinks\nfind . -type l -exec test -e {} \\; -print 2>/dev/null\n```\n\n### Rules\n\n- Verify symlinks resolve before referencing\n- Broken symlinks = context rot signal\n- Prefer direct references over symlinks\n\n---\n\n## Platform Detection Checklist\n\nWhen entering session:\n\n- [ ] Identify current platform\n- [ ] Note relevant skill paths\n- [ ] Verify symlinks resolve\n- [ ] Adjust commands for platform\n- [ ] Handle path separators correctly\n\n---\n\n## Multi-Environment Patterns\n\n### Git-Aware Discovery\n\n```bash\n# Exclude common noise\ngit ls-files --others --exclude-standard\n\n# Show tree without node_modules\nfind . -type f -not -path '*/node_modules/*' \\\n  -not -path '*/.git/*' -not -path '*/dist/*'\n```\n\n### Safe File Operations\n\n- Always use `--` to separate paths from flags\n- Quote paths with spaces\n- Use `readlink -f` for absolute paths\n",

## Created Structure

```
skills/
├── hivemind-skill-writer/           # Round 1 ✅
│   ├── SKILL.md
│   └── references/
│       ├── 01-skill-anatomy.md
│       ├── 02-frontmatter-standard.md
│       ├── 03-three-patterns.md
│       ├── 04-tdd-workflow.md
│       ├── 05-skill-quality-matrix.md
│       └── index.md
│
└── context-intelligence/             # Round 2 ✅
    ├── SKILL.md
    └── references/
        ├── 01-context-rot-taxonomy.md
        ├── 02-entry-state-matrix.md
        ├── 03-trust-matrix.md
        ├── 04-delegation-scope-rules.md
        ├── 05-platform-surface-matrix.md
        └── index.md
```

## hivemind-skill-writer (Meta-Builder)
- P1 entry skill with `stacking: 0`
- Frontmatter schema, anatomy template, 3 Patterns system
- TDD workflow, Skill-Judge quality matrix

## context-intelligence (Entry Pack)  
- P1 entry skill with `stacking: 1` (ALWAYS LOADED)
- Context rot taxonomy (0-4 severity)
- Entry state matrix (6 session states)
- Trust scoring system
- Delegation scope rules
- Cross-platform awareness

---

**Ready for reset and testing.** Once you confirm, you can load these skills and test. I'll proceed to Round 3 (Delegation-Intelligence) after confirmation.

---

## User

please for skill-writer and the project context load this skill and selectively include in hivemind-skill-writer too "npx skills add https://github.com/softaworks/agent-toolkit --skill skill-judge"

## Repository files navigation

# Softaworks Agent Skills

[](#softaworks-agent-skills)

Opinionated skills shared by [@leonardocouy](https://github.com/leonardocouy) for improving daily work efficiency with Claude Code. Skills are packaged instructions and scripts that extend agent capabilities across development, documentation, planning, and professional workflows.

Skills follow the [Agent Skills](https://agentskills.io/) format.

---

## 🧭 Quick Navigation

[](#-quick-navigation)

**[🚀 Installation](#-installation)** • **[📚 Available Skills](#-available-skills)** • **[🤖 Agents & Commands](#-agents--commands)** • **[📖 Skill Structure](#-skill-structure)** • **[🤝 Contributing](#-contributing)** • **[📄 License](#-license)** • **[🔗 Links](#-links)**

---

## 🚀 Installation

[](#-installation)

### Quick Install (Recommended)

[](#quick-install-recommended)

npx skills add softaworks/agent-toolkit

This method works with multiple AI coding agents (Claude Code, Codex, Cursor, AdaL, etc.)

### Register as Plugin Marketplace

[](#register-as-plugin-marketplace)

Run the following commands in Claude Code:

/plugin marketplace add softaworks/agent-toolkit
/plugin

### Install Plugins

[](#install-plugins)

**Option 1: Via Browse UI**

1.  Switch to **Marketplaces** tab (use arrow keys or Tab)
2.  Select **agent-toolkit**, press Enter
3.  Browse and select the plugin(s) you want to install
4.  Select **Install now**

**Option 2: Direct Install**

# Install specific skill
/plugin install codex@agent-toolkit
/plugin install humanizer@agent-toolkit

# Install specific agent
/plugin install agent-codebase-pattern-finder@agent-toolkit

# Install specific command
/plugin install command-codex-plan@agent-toolkit

**Option 3: Ask the Agent**

Simply tell Claude Code:

> Please install Skills from github.com/softaworks/agent-toolkit

### Available Plugins

[](#available-plugins)

Each skill, agent, and command is an individual plugin that can be installed separately:

-   **Skills** → See [Available Skills](#-available-skills) for the full list
-   **Agents** → See [Agents](#agents) (install as `agent-<name>@agent-toolkit`)
-   **Commands** → See [Slash Commands](#slash-commands) (install as `command-<name>@agent-toolkit`)

### Update Plugins

[](#update-plugins)

To update plugins to the latest version:

1.  Run `/plugin` in Claude Code
2.  Switch to **Marketplaces** tab
3.  Select **agent-toolkit**
4.  Choose **Update marketplace**

You can also **Enable auto-update** to get the latest versions automatically.

### Manual Installation

[](#manual-installation)

**For Claude Code (Manual)** — Skills only

cp -r skills/<skill-name\> ~/.claude/skills/

**For claude.ai** — Skills only

Add skills to project knowledge or paste SKILL.md contents into the conversation.

---

## 🤖 Agents & Commands

[](#-agents--commands)

> **Requires [Claude Code CLI](https://docs.anthropic.com/claude-code)** — These agents and commands are exclusive to Claude Code users.
> 
> For full access, add the marketplace and install plugins:
> 
> /plugin marketplace add softaworks/agent-toolkit
> /plugin install codex@agent-toolkit

### Agents

[](#agents)

Specialized sub-agents that Claude Code can delegate tasks to:

Agent

Description

ascii-ui-mockup-generator

Visualize UI concepts through ASCII mockups

codebase-pattern-finder

Find similar implementations and patterns

communication-excellence-coach

Email refinement, tone calibration, roleplay

general-purpose

Default agent for complex multi-step tasks

mermaid-diagram-specialist

Create flowcharts, sequence diagrams, ERDs

ui-ux-designer

Research-backed UI/UX design feedback

### Slash Commands

[](#slash-commands)

Reusable workflows invoked with `/command-name`:

Command

Description

`/codex-plan`

Create implementation plans using Codex 5.2

`/compose-email`

Draft professional emails

`/explain-changes-mental-model`

Build mental model of code changes

`/explain-pr-changes`

Generate PR summaries

`/sync-branch`

Sync feature branch with main

`/sync-skills-readme`

Update README skills table

`/viral-tweet`

Optimize tweet ideas for X engagement

---

## 📖 Skill Structure

[](#-skill-structure)

Each skill contains:

-   `SKILL.md` - Detailed instructions for the agent (with YAML frontmatter)
-   `README.md` - User-friendly documentation with examples
-   `scripts/` - Helper scripts for automation (optional)
-   `references/` - Supporting documentation (optional)

---

## 🤝 Contributing

[](#-contributing)

Contributions are welcome! When adding new skills:

1.  Follow the [Agent Skills](https://agentskills.io/) format
2.  Include both `SKILL.md` (for agents) and `README.md` (for users)
3.  Add YAML frontmatter to `SKILL.md` with `name:` and `description:` fields
4.  Update this README.md with a link to your skill

## About

A curated collection of skills for AI coding agents. Skills are packaged instructions and scripts that extend agent capabilities across development, documentation, planning, and professional workflows.

### Topics

[development](/topics/development "Topic: development") [automation](/topics/automation "Topic: automation") [ai](/topics/ai "Topic: ai") [claude](/topics/claude "Topic: claude") [agent-skills](/topics/agent-skills "Topic: agent-skills") [claude-code](/topics/claude-code "Topic: claude-code") [coding-agent](/topics/coding-agent "Topic: coding-agent")
